	[DESCRIPTION:A tall, half-flesh, half-plant humanoid. It has a bloom instead of a head, with a single eye set in it and a toothy mouth, an absorbed skull for protection of its brain, and a pair of flytrap-like plants on long stalks growing from its shoulders. The two flytraps are capable of injecting a venomous secretion into the blood of its victims. These beings worship primal spirits of nature, and ruthlessly decimate any who would defile the natural world.]

Formerly, they were flesh and blood, but over the years they moved to undying, mechanical bodies. Their mask-like faces are replicas of their original facial features.]
